======================== "The name speaks for itself!" ========================

                       ...AND JUSTICE FOR ALL Files List

                           http://surf.to/damage_inc
                            damage_inc@disinfo.net
===============================================================================

Introduction:  This list is *incomplete* but it contains a fair amount of the
t-files, zines, virus source code, etc. that I collected up until 1998 or so and
had available on my board.  This files list is nothing more than a capture, done
by an all files scan using my BBS software from 1995-1998, which was named
Trixter!... I still have the source code on disk somewhere.  ;)  Thankfully, I
saved almost everything on my 286 and 386 systems from that era.

First named Paradise City, I ran a board from 1989-1998 with some downtime in
between, now and again.  It was always dialup, no ratio BBS.  The amount of
users and callers varied greatly over the years.  However, I still have some
very fond memories of running AJFA, and it's an experience that I'll definitely
never forget.  Hopefully this list gives you a good idea of what type of board
it was, and what it supported.

Lastly, I'd just like to thank all of the people that supported my board during
the years that it was online.
                
The Sysop was BLACKENED.  The Co-Sysop was Shatazar.  
                                                                
I've also included a screen capture below of the file area names, just in case
people want to see how the files were organized.
